namespace=province_wealth

province_wealth.1 = {
	type = province_event
	hidden = yes
    
    trigger = {has_owner = yes}
	
	immediate = {   
        if = {
            limit = {NOT = {has_variable = province_wealth}}
            set_variable = {
                name = province_wealth
                value = 0
            }
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = province_wealth
            add = province_wealth_change
        }
        set_variable = {
            name = taxes_change
            value = taxes_change
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = province_wealth
            subtract = var:taxes_change
        }
        set_variable = {
            name = per_capita_wealth
            value = var:province_wealth
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = per_capita_wealth
            divide = total_population
        }
        set_variable = {
            name = wealth_factor
            value = wealth_factor
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = taxes_change
            multiply = tax_efficiency
        }
    }
}

        }

									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}    
            }    
        }
    }
}
